if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'd022aa3da1f3f3e9b1f513da7407fb60610f4e00') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'd022aa3da1f3f3e9b1f513da7407fb60610f4e00') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '57aa5c0d52ab9498bbee73a3eebbbcee80a53272') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'd022aa3da1f3f3e9b1f513da7407fb60610f4e00') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') != '6911f2929285c146d81282ab4894c6227b4db8ef') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== '6911f2929285c146d81282ab4894c6227b4db8ef') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'cc9a81f4b3b48bd776d506f9749a8853c14dddeb') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== '6911f2929285c146d81282ab4894c6227b4db8ef') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index_mobile.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index_mobile.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('index_mobile.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index_mobile.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index_mobile.php') != '328032af89a79c2c3d56826edb222ed9ce2eae48') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index_mobile.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index_mobile.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index_mobile.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index_mobile.php') !== '328032af89a79c2c3d56826edb222ed9ce2eae48') {
		if (@sha1_file('index_mobile.php') !== 'd5553a897a8d2351ff3f51bce9b5df9fdd0c660f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index_mobile.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index_mobile.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index_mobile.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index_mobile.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('index_mobile.php') !== '328032af89a79c2c3d56826edb222ed9ce2eae48') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index_mobile.php');
		}
	}
}
